
.. _l-onnx-doccom-microsoft-LambOptimizer:

=============================
com.microsoft - LambOptimizer
=============================

.. contents::
    :local:


.. _l-onnx-opcom-microsoft-lamboptimizer-1:

LambOptimizer - 1
=================

**Version**

* **name**: `LambOptimizer (GitHub) <https://github.com/onnx/onnx/blob/main/docs/Operators.md#com.microsoft.LambOptimizer>`_
* **domain**: **com.microsoft**
* **since_version**: **1**
* **function**:
* **support_level**: SupportType.COMMON
* **shape inference**: True

This version of the operator has been available
**since version 1 of domain com.microsoft**.

**Summary**

**Attributes**

* **alpha - FLOATS** :   Coefficient of previous gradient in running average.
* **beta - FLOATS** :   Coefficient of previous squared gradient in running average.The
  effective learning rate is computed by r = R / (1 + T *
  decay_factor). Default to 0 so that increasing update counts doesn't
  reduce the learning rate.
* **do_bias_correction - INT** :   Compute unbiased 1st and 2nd momentums.
* **epsilon - FLOATS** :   Small scalar to avoid dividing by zero.
* **lambda - FLOATS** :   Regularization coefficient of 0.5 * lambda * ||X||_2^2. Default to
  0, which means no regularization.
* **max_norm_clip - FLOATS** :   clip threshold of gradients.
* **ratio_max - FLOAT** :   Upper bound on confidence ratio.
* **ratio_min - FLOAT** :   Lower bound on confidence ratio.

**Inputs**

Between 0 and 5125 inputs.

* **update_signal** (optional, heterogeneous) - **T_BOOL**:

* **loss_scale** (optional, heterogeneous) - **T2**:

* **gradient_norm** (optional, heterogeneous) - **T_GRAD_NORM**:

* **R** (optional, heterogeneous) - **T1**:

* **step** (optional, heterogeneous) - **TInt64**:

* **__group_0__weights** (optional) - **T2**:

**Type Constraints**

* **T1** in (
  tensor(bfloat16),
  tensor(double),
  tensor(float),
  tensor(float16)
  ):
  Constrain input types to float scalars.
* **T2** in (
  tensor(double),
  tensor(float)
  ):
  Constrain input types to float tensors.
* **T3** in (
  tensor(bfloat16),
  tensor(double),
  tensor(float),
  tensor(float16)
  ):
  Constrain input types to float tensors.
* **T4** in (
  tensor(bfloat16),
  tensor(double),
  tensor(float),
  tensor(float16)
  ):
  Constrain input types to float tensors.
* **T_MIXED_PRECISION_FP** in (
  tensor(bfloat16),
  tensor(float16)
  ):
  Constrain input types to float16 or bfloat16 tensors.
* **T_GRAD_NORM** in (
  tensor(bfloat16),
  tensor(double),
  tensor(float),
  tensor(float16)
  ):
  Constrain input types to float tensors.
* **T_BOOL** in (
  tensor(bool)
  ):
  Constrain types to boolean tensors.
* **TInt64** in (
  tensor(int64)
  ):
  Constrain update count to 64-bit integer
